setTimeout(() => {
    const nextButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.framer--carousel-controls button[aria-label="Next"]');
    const prevButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.framer--carousel-controls button[aria-label="Previous"]');

    const maxLength = Math.min(nextButtons.length, prevButtons.length);
    
    for (let i = 0; i < maxLength; i++) {
        const nextButton = nextButtons[i];
        const prevButton = prevButtons[i];
        
        if (nextButton && prevButton) {
            nextButton.click();
            nextButton.style.display = 'none';
            
            setTimeout(() => {
                prevButton.click();
                prevButton.style.display = 'none';
            }, 500);
        }
    }
}, 1000);
